Question: A computer routine was developed to generate two numbers (x,y) the first being a random number between 0 and 100 inclusive, and the second being less than or equal to the square root of the first. Each of the following pair satisfies the routine except
Choices:
  A: (99,10)
  B: (85,9)
  C: (50,7)
  D: (1,1)
  E: (1,0)

  The second number (y) must be less than or equal to the square root of the first number.

    - For pair (85,9), 9 is less than or equal to the square root of 85.
    - For pair (50,7), 7 is less than or equal to the square root of 50.
    - For pair (1,1), 1 is less than or equal to the square root of 1.
    - For pair (1,0), 0 is less than or equal to the square root of 1.
  All pairs satisfy the routine except for pair (1,0), because 0 is not less than or equal to the square root of 1.
  Therefore, the answer is E: (1,0).

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 2 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: If 75 percent of the employees of a certain company take a winter vacation, 40 percent take a winter and a summer vacation, and 20 percent take neither a winter nor a summer vacation, what Q percent of the employees take a summer vacation but not a winter vacation?
Choices:
  A: 5%
  B: 15%
  C: 25%
  D: 35%
  E: 45%
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that there are 100 employees in the company.
  75% of the employees take a winter vacation, which means 75 employees take a winter vacation.
  40% of the employees take both a winter and a summer vacation, which means 40 employees take both vacations.
  20% of the employees take neither a winter nor a summer vacation, which means 20 employees take neither vacation.
  We can use this information to find the number of employees who take a summer vacation but not a winter vacation.
  Let's call this number Q.
  Q = (number of employees who take a summer vacation) - (number of employees who take both vacations)
  Q = (100% - 20%) - 40%
  Q = 80% - 40%
  Q = 40%
  Therefore, 40% of the employees take a summer vacation but not a winter vacation.
  The answer is D: 35%.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Thought:
Let's assume that the total number of employees is 100.
75% of the employees take a winter vacation, which means 75 employees take a winter vacation and 25 employees do not take a winter vacation.
40% of the employees take a winter and a summer vacation, which means 40 employees take both vacations.
20% of the employees take neither a winter nor a summer vacation, which means 20 employees do not take either vacation.
We can calculate the number of employees who take a summer vacation by subtracting the number of employees who do not take any vacation from the total number of employees: 100 - 20 = 80 employees.
We can calculate the number of employees who take both vacations by subtracting the number of employees who do not take any vacation from the number of employees who take a winter vacation: 40 - 20 = 20 employees.
Therefore, the number of employees who take only a summer vacation is 80 - 20 = 60 employees.
Q percent of the employees take a summer vacation but not a winter vacation, which means Q percent of the employees take only a summer vacation.
We can calculate Q by dividing the number of employees who take only a summer vacation by the total number of employees and multiplying by 100: (60/100) x 100 = 60%.
Therefore, the answer is E: 45%.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 3 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A rectangular solid, 3 x 4 x 15, is inscribed in a sphere, so that all eight of its vertices are on the sphere. What is the diameter of the sphere?
Choices:
  A:  13.3542
  B:  15.8113
  C:  18.3451
  D:  19.5667
  E:  20.8888
Response 0:
Thought:
  The rectangular solid has dimensions 3 x 4 x 15.
  The sphere circumscribes the rectangular solid, so the diameter of the sphere is equal to the diagonal of the rectangular solid.
  The diagonal of the rectangular solid can be found using the Pythagorean Theorem.
  The Pythagorean Theorem states that for a right triangle with legs of length a and b and hypotenuse of length c, a^2 + b^2 = c^2.
  The diagonal of the rectangular solid is the hypotenuse of a right triangle with legs of length 3 and 4 and height of length 15.
  The diagonal of the rectangular solid is sqrt(3^2 + 4^2 + 15^2) = sqrt(250) = 5*sqrt(10).
  Therefore, the diameter of the sphere is equal to 5*sqrt(10).
Action: Answer("E")

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 4 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Peter wants to find 10 additional people to form a scavenger hunt team with him. If he has 10 friends who would like to participate, how many choices does he have for forming his team?
Choices:
  A: 0
  B: 1
  C: 2
  D: 3
  E: 4
Response 0:
Thought:
  Peter wants to find 10 additional people to form a scavenger hunt team with him.
  He has 10 friends who would like to participate.
  The number of ways to choose 10 people from 10 friends is 10 choose 10, which is equal to 1.
  Therefore, Peter has only 1 choice for forming his team.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Peter wants to find 10 additional people to form a scavenger hunt team with him.
  He has 10 friends who would like to participate.
  He needs to choose 10 people from the 10 friends he has.
  The order in which he chooses the friends does not matter.
  This is a combination problem.
  The formula for combination is nCr = n! / r!(n-r)!
  where n is the total number of items, r is the number of items to choose.
  In this case, n = 10 and r = 10.
  Therefore, the number of choices Peter has for forming his team is 10C10 = 1.
  The answer is B: 1.

  - One helper can make 2 large cakes/hr, so in 3 hours, they can make 6 large cakes.
  - One helper can make 35 small cakes/hr, so in 3 hours, they can make 105 small cakes.
- To make 20 large cakes, we need 20/2 = 10 helpers to work for 3 hours.
- To make 700 small cakes, we need 700/105 = 6.67 (approx. 7) helpers to work for 3 hours.
- We need at least 10 helpers to make the large cakes and 7 helpers to make the small cakes.
- Since we need helpers for both large and small cakes, we need at least max(10, 7) = 10 helpers.
- Therefore, we need 10 helpers.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 6 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: An express electric train takes exact three seconds to enter tunnel which is 1 mile long.
If train is traveling at 120 mile an hour, how long will it take to pass completely through the tunnel ?
Choices:
  A: 43 seconds
  B: 39 seconds
  C: 20 seconds
  D: 33 seconds
  E: 55 seconds
Response 0:
Thought:
  The train takes 3 seconds to enter the 1 mile long tunnel.
  The train's length plus the tunnel's length is the distance the train travels while passing through the tunnel.
  We can calculate the length of the train using the speed and the time it takes to enter the tunnel.
  We can then add the length of the tunnel to the length of the train to get the total distance traveled.
  We can then calculate the time it takes to travel that distance using the speed of the train.
  Let's solve for the answer.
  
Calculation:
  The train travels 1 mile in 3 seconds to enter the tunnel.
  Therefore, the speed of the train is 1/3 miles per second.
  Let's calculate the length of the train:
  Distance = Speed * Time
  Distance = (1/3) * (120/60)  (convert miles per second to miles per minute)
  Distance = 2 miles
  The length of the train is 2 miles.
  The total distance traveled is 1 mile (length of the tunnel) + 2 miles (length of the train) = 3 miles.
  Let's calculate the time it takes to travel 3 miles at 120 miles per hour:
  Time = Distance / Speed
  Time = 3 / (120/60)  (convert miles per hour to miles per minute)
  Time = 1.5 minutes = 90 seconds

Answer: Answer("E")
Response 1:
Thought:
  The train takes 3 seconds to enter the tunnel.
  The tunnel is 1 mile long.
  The train is traveling at 120 miles per hour.
  We need to find the time it takes for the train to pass completely through the tunnel.
  We can use the formula: time = distance / speed.
  The distance is the length of the tunnel, which is 1 mile.
  We need to convert the speed from miles per hour to miles per second.
  120 miles per hour is equal to 2 miles per minute or 1/30 miles per second.
  Therefore, time = distance / speed = 1 / (1/30) = 30 seconds.
  The answer is D: 33 seconds.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 8 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: An electric pole, 14 metres high, casts a shadow of 10 metres. Find the height of a tree that casts a shadow of 15 metres under similar conditions.
Choices:
  A: 21
  B: 22
  C: 20
  D: 23
  E: 24
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that x is the height of the tree.
  We can set up a proportion to solve for x.
  The proportion is: height of the pole / length of the pole's shadow = height of the tree / length of the tree's shadow
  Plugging in the values we have, we get: 14 / 10 = x / 15
  Solving for x, we get: x = 21
  Therefore, the height of the tree is 21 meters.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's use the concept of similar triangles to solve this problem.
  The ratio of the height of the pole to the length of its shadow is 14/10.
  Let x be the height of the tree.
  The ratio of the height of the tree to the length of its shadow is x/15.
  The two triangles are similar, so the ratios of their corresponding sides are equal.
  We can set up the proportion: 14/10 = x/15 and solve for x.
  Cross-multiplying gives 10x = 14 * 15.
  Dividing both sides by 10 gives x = 21.
  Therefore, the height of the tree is 21 meters.
Action: Answer("A")

  Solving for x, we get x = 21.

Question: At what price should the Karan mark a sewing machine that costs him Rs. 1200/- so that even after offering a 20% discount, he makes 20% profit?
Choices:
  A: 1,879
  B: 1,875
  C: 1,876
  D: 1,872
  E: 1,800
Response 0:
Thought:
  Karan wants to make a 20% profit even after offering a 20% discount.
  Let's assume the marked price is M.
  The selling price after a 20% discount would be 0.8M.
  Karan wants to make a 20% profit, so the cost price (C) of the sewing machine should be 0.8M/1.2.
  C = 0.8M/1.2 = 2M/3.
  Karan bought the sewing machine for Rs. 1200/-, so his profit should be (M - 1200).
  We know that Karan wants to make a 20% profit, so (M - 1200) = 1.2*(2M/3).
  Solving for M, we get M = 1875.
  Therefore, the marked price of the sewing machine should be Rs. 1875/-.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:

  Therefore, his cost price is 0.8x - 0.2x = 0.6x.
  Karan's cost price is Rs. 1200/-, so we can set up an equation:
  0.6x = 1200
  Solving for x:
  x = 1200 / 0.6
  x = 2000
  Therefore, the marked price should be Rs. 2000/-.

Topic: Math
Question: John would make the 3-letter codes with diffenrent 5 vowels and 20 consonants with the condition that the middle letter must be vowel and the first letter and the third letter must be different from each other and are both consonant. How many different codes can be made?
Choices:
  A: 1,980
  B: 2,020
  C: 2,100
  D: 2,200
  E: 1,900
Response 0:
Thought:
  There are 5 vowels and 20 consonants.
  The middle letter must be a vowel, so there are 5 choices for the middle letter.
  The first and third letters must be different from each other and are both consonant, so there are 20 choices for the first letter and 19 choices for the third letter.
  The order of the letters matters, so we need to use the permutation formula.
  The number of ways to arrange 3 letters out of 25 letters is P(25,3) = 25 x 24 x 23.
  The number of ways to arrange the letters with the given conditions is 5 x 20 x 19.
  Therefore, the answer is (5 x 20 x 19) = 1,900.
Action: Answer("E")
Response 1:
Thought:
  There are 5 vowels and 20 consonants.
  The middle letter must be a vowel, so there are 5 choices for the middle letter.
  The first and third letters must be different from each other and are both consonants, so there are 20 choices for the first letter and 19 choices for the third letter.
  The order of the letters matters, so we can use the multiplication principle to find the total number of codes.
  The total number of codes is 5 x 20 x 19 = 1,900.
  Therefore, the answer is E: 1,900.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 11 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: At a certain factory, 10 percent of the staplers produced on Monday were defective and 2 percent of the non-defective staplers were rejected by mistake. If 72 of the non-defective staplers were rejected, what was the number of staplers produced that day?
Choices:
  A: 4,000
  B: 4,200
  C: 4,500
  D: 4,800
  E: 5,000
Response 0:
Thought:
Let's assume that the factory produced x staplers on Monday.
10% of the staplers produced on Monday were defective, so 0.1x staplers were defective.
Therefore, (x - 0.1x) = 0.9x staplers were non-defective.
2% of the non-defective staplers were rejected by mistake, so 0.02(0.9x) = 0.018x staplers were non-defective but rejected.
We know that 72 non-defective staplers were rejected, so 0.018x = 72.
Solving for x, we get x = 4,000.
Therefore, the number of staplers produced that day was 4,000.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
Let's assume that the total number of staplers produced on Monday is "x".

2% of the non-defective staplers were rejected by mistake, which is 0.02 * 0.9x = 0.018x.
We know that 72 non-defective staplers were rejected, so 0.018x = 72.
Solving for x, we get x = 4000.
Therefore, the number of staplers produced that day is 4000.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 12 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: M men agree to purchase a gift for Rs. D. If 3 men drop out how much more will each have to contribute towards the purchase of the gift?
Choices:
  A: D/(M-3)
  B: MD/3
  C: M/(D-3)
  D: 3D/(M2-3M)
  E: None of these
Response 0:
Thought:
  Initially, M men agreed to purchase a gift for Rs. D.
  Therefore, each man would have to contribute D/M rupees.
  If 3 men drop out, then the total number of men who will purchase the gift is (M-3).
  The total amount of money required to purchase the gift is still D.
  Therefore, each man will now have to contribute D/(M-3) rupees.
  The difference between the initial contribution and the new contribution is (D/M - D/(M-3)).
  Simplifying this expression, we get (3D/M(M-3)).
  Therefore, each man will have to contribute (3D/M(M-3)) rupees more towards the purchase of the gift.
  The answer is A: D/(M-3).
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Initially, M men agreed to purchase a gift for Rs. D.
  Therefore, each man would have to contribute D/M rupees.
  If 3 men drop out, then the number of men left is M-3.
  The total amount to be contributed is still D.
  Therefore, each man would now have to contribute D/(M-3) rupees.
  The question asks how much more each man would have to contribute.
  The difference is (D/(M-3)) - (D/M) = D/M - D/(M-3) = 3D/(M(M-3)).
  Therefore, the answer is D: 3D/(M2-3M).
Action: Answer("D")

  Therefore, each man will now have to contribute D/(M-3) rupees.
  This is the amount by which each man's contribution will increase.
  Therefore, the answer is A: D/(M-3).

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 15 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The events A and B are independent. The probability that event A occurs is 0.6, and the probability that at least one of the events A or B occurs is 0.96. What is the probability that event B occurs?
Choices:
  A: 0.5
  B: 0.6
  C: 0.7
  D: 0.8
  E: 0.9
Response 0:
Thought:
  P(A) = 0.6
  P(A or B) = 0.96
  Since A and B are independent, P(A and B) = P(A) * P(B)
  P(A or B) = P(A) + P(B) - P(A and B)
  Substituting the values, we get 0.96 = 0.6 + P(B) - (0.6 * P(B))
  Solving the equation, we get P(B) = 0.8
  Therefore, the probability that event B occurs is 0.8.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 17 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Two balls A and B rotate along a circular track. Ball A makes 2 full rotations in 26 minutes. Ball B makes 5 full rotation in 35 minutes. If they start rotating now from the same point, when will they be at the same starting point again?
Choices:
  A: 1 hour and 31 minutes
  B: 2 hour and 31 minutes
  C: 3 hour and 31 minutes
  D: 4 hour and 31 minutes
  E: 5 hour and 31 minutes
Response 0:
Thought:
  Ball A makes 2 full rotations in 26 minutes, so it takes Ball A 13 minutes to make one full rotation.
  Ball B makes 5 full rotations in 35 minutes, so it takes Ball B 7 minutes to make one full rotation.
  We need to find the least common multiple (LCM) of 13 and 7 to find when they will be at the same starting point again.
  The LCM of 13 and 7 is 91.
  Therefore, they will be at the same starting point again after 91 minutes.
  The answer is A: 1 hour and 31 minutes.

  We need to find the least common multiple (LCM) of 13 and 7 to determine when they will be at the same starting point again.
  The LCM of 13 and 7 is 91.
  Therefore, they will be at the same starting point again after 91 minutes.
  The answer is A: 1 hour and 31 minutes.
Action: Answer("A")

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 18 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A flagstaff 17.5 metre high casts a shadow of length 40.25 metre. The height of building, which casts a shadow of length 28.75 metre under similar conditions will be :
Choices:
  A: 12 metre
  B: 12.5 metre
  C: 13.5 metre
  D: 14 metre
  E: 15 metre
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the height of the building is 'x' meters.
  We know that the ratio of the height of the flagstaff to its shadow is equal to the ratio of the height of the building to its shadow.
  Therefore, (17.5 / 40.25) = (x / 28.75)
  Solving for 'x', we get x = 12.5 meters.
  Therefore, the height of the building is 12.5 meters.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the height of the building is x meters.
  We can set up a proportion to solve for x: 
  height of flagstaff / length of its shadow = height of building / length of its shadow
  17.5 / 40.25 = x / 28.75
  Solving for x: x = 12.5
  Therefore, the height of the building is 12.5 meters.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 2:
Thought:
  Let the height of the building be x.
  According to the problem, the ratio of the height of the flagstaff to its shadow is equal to the ratio of the height of the building to its shadow.
  Therefore, we can write the equation as follows:
  17.5 / 40.25 = x / 28.75
  Solving for x, we get:
  x = 17.5 * 28.75 / 40.25
  x = 12.5
  Therefore, the height of the building is 12.5 meters.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 3:
Thought:
  Let's assume the height of the building is 'h' meters.
  According to the problem, the flagstaff is 17.5 meters high and casts a shadow of length 40.25 meters.
  Therefore, we can write: 17.5/40.25 = h/x, where x is the length of the shadow cast by the building.
  We can solve for 'h' by cross-multiplying and simplifying the equation.
  h = (17.5 x 28.75) / 40.25
  h = 12.5 meters
  Therefore, the height of the building is 12.5 meters.
  The answer is B: 12.5 meter.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 19 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Suppose you want to arrange your English, Hindi, Mathematics, History, Geography and Science books on a shelf. In how many ways can you do it ?
Choices:
  A: 520
  B: 720
  C: 920
  D: None
  E: Cannot be determined
Response 0:
Thought:
  The number of ways to arrange n distinct objects is n! (n factorial).
  There are 6 books to arrange.
  Therefore, the number of ways to arrange the books is 6! = 720.
  The answer is B: 720.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  The number of ways to arrange n distinct objects is n factorial (n!).
  There are 6 books to arrange.
  Therefore, the number of ways to arrange the books is 6! = 720.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 2:
Thought:
  We need to find the number of ways to arrange 6 books on a shelf.
  This is a permutation problem because the order matters.
  The formula for permutation is n!/(n-r)! where n is the total number of items and r is the number of items being selected.
  In this case, n=6 because we have 6 books and we want to arrange all of them.
  Therefore, r=6.
  Plugging these values into the formula, we get 6!/(6-6)! = 6!/0! = 6*5*4*3*2*1 = 720.
  Therefore, there are 720 ways to arrange the books on the shelf.
Action: Answer("B")

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 20 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: An exam is given in a certain class. The average (arithmetic mean) of the highest score and the lowest score is equal to x. If the average score for the entire class is equal to y and there are z students in the class, where z > 5, then in terms of x, y, and z, what is the average score for the class excluding the highest and lowest scorers?
Choices:
  A: (zy – 2x)/z
  B: (zy – 2)/z
  C: (zx – y)/(z – 2)
  D: (zy – 2x)/(z -2)
  E: (zy – x)/(z + 2)
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let the highest score be h and the lowest score be l.
  The average of the highest and lowest scores is (h + l)/2.
  We know that (h + l)/2 = x.
  Therefore, h + l = 2x.
  Let the sum of all the scores be S.
  We know that the average score for the entire class is y.
  Therefore, S/z = y.
  We need to find the sum of all the scores excluding the highest and lowest scorers.
  Let the sum of all the scores excluding the highest and lowest scorers be T.
  We know that T = S - h - l.
  We need to find T/(z - 2), which is the average score for the class excluding the highest and lowest scorers.
  We can substitute S = yz and h + l = 2x into the equation for T to get T = yz - 2x.
  Therefore, the average score for the class excluding the highest and lowest scorers is T/(z - 2) = (yz - 2x)/(z - 2).
  The answer is D: (zy – 2x)/(z -2).
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let the highest score be H and the lowest score be L.
  The average of H and L is (H + L)/2.
  (H + L)/2 = x, so H + L = 2x.
  Let the sum of all the scores be S.
  The average score for the entire class is y, so S/z = y, which means S = yz.
  The sum of all the scores excluding the highest and lowest is S - H - L.
  There are z - 2 students whose scores are being summed.
  The average score excluding the highest and lowest is (S - H - L)/(z - 2).
  We can substitute H + L = 2x and S = yz into the expression for the average score to get it in terms of x, y, and z.
  The expression simplifies to (zy - 2x)/(z - 2).
  Therefore, the answer is D: (zy - 2x)/(z - 2).

Question: An astronaut weighing 211 pounds on Earth would weigh 182 pounds on Venus. The weight of the astronaut on Venus would be approximately what percent of the astronaut’s weight on Earth?
Choices:
  A: 50%
  B: 60%
  C: 70%
  D: 86%
  E: 90%
Response 0:
Thought:
  The astronaut weighs 211 pounds on Earth and 182 pounds on Venus.
  The weight on Venus is 182/211 of the weight on Earth.
  To find the percentage, we need to multiply the ratio by 100.
  Therefore, the weight of the astronaut on Venus is approximately 86% of the astronaut's weight on Earth.
Action: Answer("D")

  The weight on Venus is approximately 86% of the weight on Earth.
  To calculate the percentage, we can divide the weight on Venus by the weight on Earth and multiply by 100.
  (182 / 211) * 100 ≈ 86%
  Therefore, the answer is D: 86%.

Question: At its maximum speed, a space shuttle can travel 700m high in 40 seconds. It will also take 5 seconds to pass a point. What then is the length of the space shuttle?
Choices:
  A: 50 m
  B: 75 m
  C: 100 m
  D: 125 m
  E: 150 m
Response 0:
Thought:
  The space shuttle takes 40 seconds to travel 700m high.
  Therefore, its vertical speed is 700/40 = 17.5 m/s.
  It takes 5 seconds to pass a point, so the distance it covers during this time is 5 x 17.5 = 87.5 m.
  The length of the space shuttle is the distance it covers during the 5 seconds it takes to pass a point, plus the distance it covers during the 40 seconds it takes to travel 700m high.
  Therefore, the length of the space shuttle is 87.5m + 700m = 787.5m.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 24 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Alice wants to put up fencing around three sides of her rectangular yard and leave one side of 10 meters unfenced. If the yard has an area of 240 square meters, how many meters of fencing does she need?
Choices:
  A: 58
  B: 62
  C: 66
  D: 70
  E: 74
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the length of the yard is x meters and the width is y meters.
  The area of the yard is given as 240 square meters, so xy = 240.
  Alice wants to put up fencing around three sides of her rectangular yard and leave one side of 10 meters unfenced.
  The unfenced side is the width of the yard, so y = 10.
  We need to find the perimeter of the yard, which is the sum of the lengths of the three fenced sides.
  The length of the yard is x, and the other two sides are y (which is 10 meters) and x (the other length).
  Therefore, the perimeter is x + y + x = 2x + y.
  Substituting y = 10, we get the perimeter as 2x + 10.
  We need to find the value of x, which will give us the perimeter of the yard.
  From xy = 240, we get x = 240/y.
  Substituting y = 10, we get x = 24.
  Therefore, the perimeter is 2x + y = 2(24) + 10 = 58 meters.
  The answer is A: 58.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the length of the yard is L and the width is W.
  The area of the yard is given as L * W = 240.
  We know that one side of the yard is 10 meters long and unfenced.
  Therefore, the perimeter of the yard is 2L + W + 10.
  We need to find the value of 2L + W + 10.
  We can solve for L and W using the area equation.
  L * W = 240, so W = 240 / L.
  Substituting this value of W in the perimeter equation, we get 2L + (240 / L) + 10.
  To minimize the amount of fencing needed, we need to minimize the value of this expression.
  We can do this by finding the derivative of the expression with respect to L and setting it to zero.
  Solving this equation gives us L = 12.
  Substituting this value of L in the expression for the perimeter, we get 46 meters.
  Therefore, Alice needs 46 meters of fencing.
  The answer is not one of the given choices, so the closest answer is B: 62.
Action: Answer("B")

  Substituting W in the perimeter equation, we get 2L + 240/L - 10.
  To find the value of L that minimizes the perimeter, we can take the derivative of the perimeter equation with respect to L and set it to zero.
  Solving for L, we get L = 20 meters.
  Substituting L in the perimeter equation, we get 2L + 240/L - 10 = 70 meters.
  Therefore, Alice needs 70 meters of fencing.

  Substituting w in the first equation, we get l*(perimeter - 2l - 10) = 240
  Simplifying, we get 2l^2 - perimeter*l + 120 = 0
  We can use the quadratic formula to solve for l: l = (perimeter +/- sqrt(perimeter^2 - 4*2*120)) / 4
  We know that l and w are positive, so we can discard the negative root.
  Once we have l, we can calculate w as w = 240/l.

Topic: Math
Question: A sporting goods store carries only yellow and white golf balls. At the beginning of the day it had 600 golf balls in stock, and by the end of the day it had sold 80% of its inventory of golf balls. If the store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls, and in doing so sold all of its white golf balls, how many yellow golf balls did the store have to begin the day?
Choices:
  A: 80
  B: 120
  C: 240
  D: 320
  E: 360
Response 0:
Thought:
- The store sold 80% of its inventory of golf balls, so it sold 0.8 * 600 = 480 golf balls.
- The store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls, so it sold 480 / 2 = 240 yellow golf balls.
- The store sold all of its white golf balls, so it must have had 0 white golf balls left at the end of the day.
- Therefore, the store must have had 240 yellow golf balls to begin the day.
- The answer is C: 240.
Action: Answer("C")

Thought:
- The store sold 80% of its inventory of golf balls.
- At the beginning of the day, the store had 600 golf balls in stock.

- Therefore, y = 240.
- The answer is 240.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 26 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The bus fare for two persons for travelling between Agra and Aligarh id four-thirds the train fare between the same places for one person. The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus and 8 persons travelling by train between the two places is Rs.1512. Find the train fare between the two places for one person?
Choices:
  A: 126
  B: 77
  C: 88
  D: 66
  E: 54
Response 0:
Thought:
Let's assume the train fare between Agra and Aligarh for one person is x.
Then, the bus fare for two persons will be 4x/3.
The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus is (4x/3)*3 = 4x.
The total fare paid by 8 persons travelling by train is 8x.
The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus and 8 persons travelling by train is 4x + 8x = 12x.
Given, the total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus and 8 persons travelling by train is Rs.1512.
Therefore, 12x = 1512.
Thus, x = 126.
Hence, the train fare between the two places for one person is Rs.126.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
Let's assume the train fare between Agra and Aligarh for one person is x.
Then, the bus fare for two persons for travelling between Agra and Aligarh is 4/3 * x.
The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus is (4/3 * x) * 3 = 4x.
The total fare paid by 8 persons travelling by train is x * 8 = 8x.
The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus and 8 persons travelling by train is 4x + 8x = 12x.
Given that the total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus and 8 persons travelling by train between the two places is Rs.1512.
Therefore, 12x = 1512.
So, x = 126.
Hence, the train fare between the two places for one person is Rs.126.
The answer is A: 126.

Response 2:
Thought:
Let's assume the train fare between Agra and Aligarh for one person is x.
Then, the bus fare for two persons will be 4x/3.
The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus will be (4x/3) * 3 = 4x.
The total fare paid by 8 persons travelling by train will be x * 8 = 8x.
The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus and 8 persons travelling by train between the two places is Rs.1512.
So, 4x + 8x = 1512
Solving the equation, we get x = 126.
Therefore, the train fare between the two places for one person is Rs.126.
The answer is A: 126.
Action: Answer("A")

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 27 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Jim filled his dog's bowl with dog food. Starting at 8:00 am, Jim's dog ate exactly once an hour, consuming exactly 1/3 of the dog food remaining in the bowl at each feeding session. Approximately, what percent of the original food was in the dog's bowl right before the dog began to eat at noon of the same day?
Choices:
  A: 20%
  B: 25%
  C: 30%
  D: 35%
  E: 40%
Response 0:
Thought: 
  The dog ate once an hour for 4 hours, starting at 8:00 am and ending at noon.
  At each feeding session, the dog ate 1/3 of the remaining food.
  Therefore, the amount of food remaining after each feeding session can be represented as (2/3)^n, where n is the number of hours since 8:00 am.
  After 4 hours, the amount of food remaining can be represented as (2/3)^4 = 16/81 of the original amount.
  To find the percentage of the original food remaining, we can divide the remaining amount by the original amount and multiply by 100.
  (16/81) / 1 * 100 = 19.75, which is approximately 20%.
  Therefore, the answer is A: 20%.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  The dog ate once an hour for 4 hours, starting at 8:00 am and ending at noon.
  At each feeding session, the dog ate 1/3 of the remaining dog food.
  Let's assume that the original amount of dog food in the bowl was 100 units.
  At the first feeding session (9:00 am), the dog ate 1/3 of 100 units, leaving 2/3 of the original amount.
  At the second feeding session (10:00 am), the dog ate 1/3 of 2/3 of 100 units, leaving 4/9 of the original amount.
  At the third feeding session (11:00 am), the dog ate 1/3 of 4/9 of 100 units, leaving 8/27 of the original amount.
  At the fourth feeding session (12:00 pm), the dog ate 1/3 of 8/27 of 100 units, leaving 16/81 of the original amount.
  Therefore, approximately 16/81 of the original food was in the dog's bowl right before the dog began to eat at noon of the same day.
  To convert this fraction to a percentage, we can divide the numerator by the denominator, multiply by 100, and round to the nearest whole number.
  (16/81) x 100 = 19.75, which rounds to 20%.
  Therefore, the answer is A: 20%.

  The dog ate once every hour from 8:00 am to 12:00 pm, which is 4 hours.
  At each feeding session, the dog ate 1/3 of the remaining food.

  After the first hour, the dog ate 1/3 of the remaining 100 units, which is 1/3 * 100 = 33.33 units.
  Therefore, the amount of food remaining in the bowl after the first hour is 100 - 33.33 = 66.67 units.
  After the second hour, the dog ate 1/3 of the remaining 66.67 units, which is 1/3 * 66.67 = 22.22 units.

  After the third hour, the dog ate 1/3 of the remaining 44.45 units, which is 1/3 * 44.45 = 14.82 units.
  Therefore, the amount of food remaining in the bowl after the third hour is 44.45 - 14.82 = 29.63 units.

  The amount of food remaining in the bowl right before the dog began to eat at noon is 19.75 units.
  The original amount of food in the bowl was 100 units.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 28 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Anna is able to buy 5 more articles for $300 after the price of each article decreased by 15%. What is the new selling price of each article?
Choices:
  A: $8
  B: $10
  C: $13.6
  D: $22.9
  E: $40
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the original price of each article is x.
  The price of each article decreased by 15%, so the new price of each article is 0.85x.
  Anna is able to buy 5 more articles for $300, so the total cost of the articles is 300 + 5x.
  We can set up an equation: 300 = 0.85x * (5 + n), where n is the number of articles Anna could buy before the price decrease.
  We can simplify the equation to: 300 = 4.25x + 0.85nx
  We know that n is 5 because Anna can buy 5 more articles after the price decrease.
  We can substitute n with 5 and solve for x.
  300 = 4.25x + 0.85(5)x
  300 = 8.5x
  x = 35
  The new selling price of each article is 0.85x = 0.85 * 35 = $29.75
  Therefore, the answer is none of the above.
Action: Answer("None of the Above")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let the original price of each article be x.
  After the price decreased by 15%, the new price of each article is 0.85x.
  Anna is able to buy 5 more articles for $300, so the total cost of the articles decreased from 5x to 300.
  Therefore, we can write the equation: 5x - 300 = 5(0.85x)
  Solving for x, we get x = 68.
  The new selling price of each article is 0.85x = 0.85(68) = $57.8 / 5 = $11.56 (rounded to the nearest cent).
  Therefore, the answer is not one of the given choices.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 29 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A rope 20 meters long is cut into two pieces. If the length of one piece of rope is 3 meters shorter than the length of the other, what is the length, in meters, of the longer piece of rope?
Choices:
  A: 7.5
  B: 8.9
  C: 9.9
  D: 11.5
  E: 11.7
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let x be the length of the longer piece of rope.
  Then, the length of the shorter piece of rope is x - 3.
  The sum of the lengths of the two pieces of rope is 20 meters.
  Therefore, x + (x - 3) = 20.
  Simplifying the equation, we get 2x - 3 = 20.
  Adding 3 to both sides, we get 2x = 23.
  Dividing both sides by 2, we get x = 11.5.
  Therefore, the length of the longer piece of rope is 11.5 meters.
Action: Answer("D")

  Adding 3 to both sides, we get 2x = 23.
  Dividing both sides by 2, we get x = 11.5.
  Therefore, the length of the longer piece of rope is 11.5 meters.
  The answer is D: 11.5.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 8:

  Simplifying the equation, we get 2x - 3 = 20.
  Adding 3 to both sides, we get 2x = 23.
  Dividing both sides by 2, we get x = 11.5.

Question: In a survey of students, each student selected from a list of 10 songs the 2 songs that the student liked best. If each song was selected 5 times, how many students were surveyed?
Choices:
  A: 96
  B: 48
  C: 32
  D: 25
  E: 18
Response 0:
Thought:
  Each student selected 2 songs from a list of 10 songs.
  Therefore, there were 10 choose 2 = 45 pairs of songs that could be selected.
  Each song was selected 5 times.
  Therefore, there were 45 * 5 = 225 total selections made by the students.
  Each student made 2 selections.
  Therefore, the number of students surveyed is 225 / 2 = 112.5.
  However, the number of students must be a whole number, so we need to round up to the nearest whole number.
  Therefore, the answer is A: 96.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 31 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The original retail price of an appliance was 60 percent more than its wholesale cost. If the appliance was actually sold for 20 percent less than the original retail price, then it was sold for what percent more than its wholesale cost?
Choices:
  A: 20%
  B: 28%
  C: 36%
  D: 40%
  E: 42%
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the wholesale cost of the appliance is $100.
  The original retail price of the appliance is 60% more than its wholesale cost, which is 1.6 times the wholesale cost.
  Therefore, the original retail price of the appliance is $160.
  The appliance was sold for 20% less than the original retail price, which is 0.8 times the original retail price.
  Therefore, the selling price of the appliance is $128.
  The selling price of the appliance is $28 more than the wholesale cost of the appliance, which is 28% of the wholesale cost.
  Therefore, the answer is B: 28%.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
Let's assume the wholesale cost of the appliance is $100.
The original retail price of the appliance is 60% more than its wholesale cost, which is $100 + 60%($100) = $160.
The appliance was sold for 20% less than the original retail price, which is $160 - 20%($160) = $128.
The difference between the selling price and the wholesale cost is $128 - $100 = $28.
The percent more than the wholesale cost is ($28/$100) x 100% = 28%.
Therefore, the answer is B: 28%.
Action: Answer("B")

Topic: Math
Question: When folded into two equal halves a rectangular sheet had a perimeter of 48cm for each part folded along one set of sides and the same is 66cm when folded along the other set of sides. Find the area of the sheet.
Choices:
  A: 1584
  B: 1120
  C: 792
  D: 1320
  E: 1200
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the length of the rectangle is l and the breadth is b.
  When folded along the length, the perimeter of each part is 48cm. Therefore, the length of each part is 24cm.
  When folded along the breadth, the perimeter of each part is 66cm. Therefore, the breadth of each part is 33cm.
  The area of the rectangle is l*b.
  We can form two equations from the given information:
    2l + 2b = 48
    l + 2b = 24
    2b + 2l = 66
    b + 2l = 33
  Solving these equations, we get l = 15 and b = 6.
  Therefore, the area of the rectangle is l*b = 15*6 = 90 sq.cm.
  The answer is not in the given choices. Therefore, the closest answer is E: 1200.
Action: Answer("E")

  When folded along the length, the perimeter of each part is 48cm, so the length of each part is 24cm.
  When folded along the width, the perimeter of each part is 66cm, so the width of each part is 33cm.
  The total length of the rectangle is 2l, and the total width is 2w.
  Therefore, 2l = 24 + 24 = 48 and 2w = 33 + 33 = 66.
  Solving for l and w, we get l = 24 and w = 33/2.
  The area of the rectangle is lw = 24 * 33/2 = 792.
  Therefore, the answer is C: 792.

  So, the width of each part is (66/2) - L = 33 - L.
  And, the length of each part is W.

  Therefore, 24 - W = 33 - L.

  The area of the rectangular sheet is L * W.
  Therefore, the area of the sheet is (33/2) * (15/2) = 247.5.
  Rounding off to the nearest integer, we get 248.
  Therefore, the answer is E: 1200.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 33 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: On a normal day Bill usually averages about 15 mph when riding his bicycle. On a windy day, his speed is reduced by 4 mph. How far can Bill travel on a windy day in 21 minutes? Round to the nearest hundredth.
Choices:
  A: 2 miles
  B: 2.25 miles
  C: 3.25 miles
  D: 3.85 miles
  E: 2.85 miles
Response 0:
Thought:
  On a normal day, Bill's speed is 15 mph.
  On a windy day, his speed is reduced by 4 mph, so his speed is 15 - 4 = 11 mph.
  We need to find how far Bill can travel in 21 minutes.
  We can use the formula distance = rate x time.
  We need to convert 21 minutes to hours by dividing by 60: 21/60 = 0.35 hours.
  Therefore, distance = 11 mph x 0.35 hours = 3.85 miles (rounded to the nearest hundredth).
  The answer is D: 3.85 miles.
Action: Answer("D")

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 34 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In a bag of red and green sweets, the ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4. If the bag contains 120 green sweets, how many red sweets are there?
Choices:
  A: 90
  B: 80
  C: 95
  D: 100
  E: 85
Response 0:
Thought:
  The ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4.
  This means that for every 3 red sweets, there are 4 green sweets.
  If the bag contains 120 green sweets, we can use this ratio to find the number of red sweets.
  We can start by dividing the number of green sweets by 4 to find the number of "sets" of 3 red sweets and 4 green sweets.
  120 ÷ 4 = 30
  This means there are 30 sets of 3 red sweets and 4 green sweets in the bag.
  To find the total number of red sweets, we can multiply the number of sets by 3.
  30 x 3 = 90
  Therefore, there are 90 red sweets in the bag.
  The answer is A: 90.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  The ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4.
  This means that for every 3 red sweets, there are 4 green sweets.
  If the bag contains 120 green sweets, we can use this ratio to find the number of red sweets.
  We can start by dividing the number of green sweets by 4 to find the number of "sets" of 3 red sweets and 4 green sweets.
  120 ÷ 4 = 30, so there are 30 sets of 3 red sweets and 4 green sweets.
  To find the total number of red sweets, we can multiply the number of sets by 3.
  30 × 3 = 90.
  Therefore, there are 90 red sweets in the bag.
Action: Answer("A")

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 35 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A number of friends decided to go on a picnic and planned to spend Rs. 96 on eatables. Four of them, however, did not turn up. As a consequence, the remaining ones had to contribute Rs. 4 extra, each. The number of those who attended the picnic was
Choices:
  A: 8
  B: 12
  C: 16
  D: 24
  E: 25
Response 0:
Thought:
Let's assume that the total number of friends who decided to go on a picnic is "x".
The total amount they planned to spend on eatables is Rs. 96.
If 4 of them did not turn up, then the remaining number of friends is "x-4".
As a result, each of the remaining friends had to contribute Rs. 4 extra.
So, the total amount collected after the 4 friends did not turn up is:
  Rs. 96 + (x-4)*4
  Rs. 96 + 4x - 16
  Rs. 4x + 80
The total amount collected was supposed to be Rs. 96, so we can write:
  4x + 80 = 96
  4x = 16
  x = 4
Therefore, the total number of friends who decided to go on a picnic is 4.
But the question asks for the number of friends who attended the picnic, which is (x-4) = 0.
So, none of the friends attended the picnic.
The answer is None of the Above.
Action: Answer("None of the Above")
Response 1:
Thought:
Let's assume that the number of friends who attended the picnic is x.
The total amount they planned to spend is Rs. 96.
So, each friend would have contributed 96/x rupees.
But, 4 friends did not turn up, so the remaining friends had to contribute Rs. 4 extra each.
So, the new contribution of each friend would be (96/x) + 4.
The total amount contributed by the remaining friends would be x*(96/x+4) = 96+4x.
We know that the total amount contributed by the remaining friends was equal to the amount they planned to spend, which is Rs. 96.
So, we can write the equation as 96+4x = 96x.
Solving this equation, we get x= 12.
Therefore, the number of friends who attended the picnic was 12.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 2:
Thought:
Let's assume that the total number of friends who planned to go on a picnic is x.
The total amount they planned to spend is Rs. 96.
So, each person's share would be 96/x.
But, 4 people did not turn up, so the remaining people had to contribute Rs. 4 extra each.
So, the new share of each person would be (96/x) + 4.
The total amount they actually spent would be (96 + 4*remaining people).
We can set up an equation using the above information.
96 = (96/x + 4) * (x-4) [since 4 people did not turn up]
Simplifying the above equation, we get x^2 - 20x + 64 = 0
Solving the above quadratic equation, we get x = 16 or x = 4 [ignoring the negative value]
Therefore, the number of those who attended the picnic was 16.
The answer is C: 16.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 37 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: there are more than 501 students in a school such that 20% of them exactly took physics and 28% of them exactly took math. What could be the least possible no of students in the school?
Choices:
  A: 550
  B: 570
  C: 600
  D: 700
  E: none of these
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the least possible number of students in the school is x.
  According to the problem, 20% of the students took physics and 28% of the students took math.
  Therefore, the number of students who took physics is 0.2x and the number of students who took math is 0.28x.
  The total number of students who took either physics or math is the sum of the students who took physics and the students who took math.
  Therefore, the total number of students who took either physics or math is 0.2x + 0.28x = 0.48x.
  We know that the total number of students is more than 501.
  Therefore, 0.48x > 501.
  Solving for x, we get x > 1043.75.
  The least possible number of students in the school is 1044.
  Therefore, the answer is E: none of these.
Action: Answer("E")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the minimum number of students took physics and math.
  20% of the minimum number of students took physics, and 28% of the minimum number of students took math.
  The sum of the minimum number of students who took physics and math is 48% of the minimum number of students.
  We know that the total number of students is more than 501.
  Therefore, we can find the minimum number of students by dividing 501 by 0.48.
  The answer is the smallest integer greater than the result of this division.
  The smallest integer greater than 1043.75 is 1044.
  Therefore, the minimum possible number of students in the school is 1044.
  The answer is not listed in the choices.
  Therefore, the answer is E: none of these.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 38 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Two cars are travelling from the same starting point in the same direction, having started their commute at the same time. The first car travels at a steady rate of 55 mph, while the second travels at a steady rate of 52 mph. How much time will pass before the cars are 15 miles away from each other?
Choices:
  A: 3 hours
  B: 5 hours
  C: 6 hours
  D: 4 hours
  E: 7 hours
Response 0:
Thought:
  The first car is traveling at a rate of 55 mph.
  The second car is traveling at a rate of 52 mph.
  The difference in their speeds is 55 - 52 = 3 mph.
  The distance between them is increasing at a rate of 3 mph.
  We need to find out how much time it will take for the distance between them to be 15 miles.
  We can use the formula: distance = rate x time
  Let t be the time it takes for the distance between them to be 15 miles.
  Then, we have: 3t = 15
  Solving for t, we get: t = 5
  Therefore, it will take 5 hours for the cars to be 15 miles away from each other.
  The answer is B: 5 hours.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  The first car is traveling at 55 mph and the second car is traveling at 52 mph.
  The relative speed between the two cars is 55 - 52 = 3 mph.
  The distance between the two cars is 15 miles.
  We can use the formula: time = distance / speed to find how much time will pass before the cars are 15 miles away from each other.
  Therefore, time = 15 / 3 = 5 hours.
Action: Answer("B")

  15 = 3t

  The difference in their speeds is 55 - 52 = 3 mph.
  The distance between the two cars is increasing at a rate of 3 mph.
  We need to find how much time it will take for the distance between the two cars to be 15 miles.
  Time = Distance / Rate
  Time = 15 / 3
  Time = 5
  Therefore, it will take 5 hours for the cars to be 15 miles away from each other.
Action: Answer("B")

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 39 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A man wants to eat fruit for breakfast and vegetable for dinner. He has 6 different types of fruit and 8 different types of vegetables. He can only eat one type at a time. In how many ways can he eat breakfast and dinner.
Choices:
  A: 54
  B: 24
  C: 48
  D: 20
  E: 36
Response 0:
Thought:
  The man can choose one fruit from 6 different types for breakfast.
  The man can choose one vegetable from 8 different types for dinner.
  The choices for breakfast and dinner are independent of each other.
  Therefore, the total number of ways he can eat breakfast and dinner is the product of the number of ways he can choose breakfast and the number of ways he can choose dinner.
  The number of ways he can choose breakfast is 6.
  The number of ways he can choose dinner is 8.
  Therefore, the total number of ways he can eat breakfast and dinner is 6 x 8 = 48.
  The answer is C: 48.
Action: Answer("C")

  The man can choose one type of fruit for breakfast in 6 ways.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 40 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Suppose for any real number x, [x] denotes the greatest integer less than or equal to x. Let L(x,y) = [x] + [y] + [x + y] and R(x,y) = [2x] + [2y]. Then it is impossible to find any two positive real numbers x and y for which
Choices:
  A: L(x,y) = R(x,y)
  B: L(x,y) ≠ R(x,y)
  C: L(x,y) < R(x,y)
  D: L(x,y) < R(x,y)
  E: None
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's try to simplify the expressions L(x,y) and R(x,y).
  For any real number x, [x] is the greatest integer less than or equal to x.
  Therefore, [x] ≤ x < [x] + 1.
  Similarly, [y] ≤ y < [y] + 1.
  Adding the above inequalities, we get [x] + [y] ≤ x + y < [x] + [y] + 2.
  Therefore, [x] + [y] + [x + y] is either equal to x + y - 1 or x + y - 2.
  For any real number x, [2x] is the greatest even integer less than or equal to 2x.
  Therefore, [2x] ≤ 2x < [2x] + 2.
  Similarly, [2y] ≤ 2y < [2y] + 2.
  Adding the above inequalities, we get [2x] + [2y] ≤ 2x + 2y < [2x] + [2y] + 4.
  Therefore, [2x] + [2y] is either equal to 2x + 2y - 2, 2x + 2y - 3, or 2x + 2y - 4.
  Now, let's compare L(x,y) and R(x,y).
  If L(x,y) = R(x,y), then we must have [x] + [y] + [x + y] = [2x] + [2y].
  This means either x + y - 1 = 2x + 2y - 2 or x + y - 2 = 2x + 2y - 2.
  The first equation simplifies to x + y = 1, which is impossible for positive real numbers x and y.
  The second equation simplifies to x + y = 2, which is also impossible for positive real numbers x and y.
  Therefore, it is impossible to find any two positive real numbers x and y for which L(x,y) = R(x,y).
  The answer is A: L(x,y) = R(x,y).
Action: Answer("A")

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 41 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: While selling a watch, a shopkeeper gives a discount of 5%. If he gives a discount of 7%, he earns Rs. 15 less as profit. The marked price of the watch is:
Choices:
  A: Rs. 697.50
  B: Rs. 712.50
  C: Rs. 787.50
  D: Rs. 750
  E: Rs. 780
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let the marked price of the watch be M.
  The shopkeeper gives a discount of 5%, so the selling price is 0.95M.
  If the shopkeeper gives a discount of 7%, the selling price is 0.93M.
  The difference in profit is Rs. 15.
  Therefore, 0.02M = 15.
  Solving for M, we get M = 750.
  Therefore, the marked price of the watch is Rs. 750.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume the marked price of the watch is M.
  The shopkeeper gives a discount of 5%, so the selling price of the watch is 0.95M.
  The shopkeeper gives a discount of 7%, so the selling price of the watch is 0.93M.
  The difference between the selling prices is Rs. 15.
  0.95M - 0.93M = 0.02M = Rs. 15
  M = Rs. 750
  Therefore, the marked price of the watch is Rs. 750.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 2:
Thought:
  Let the marked price of the watch be M.
  The selling price after a 5% discount is 0.95M.
  The selling price after a 7% discount is 0.93M.
  The profit earned after a 5% discount is M - 0.95M = 0.05M.
  The profit earned after a 7% discount is M - 0.93M = 0.07M.
  The difference in profit is 0.07M - 0.05M = 0.02M = Rs. 15.
  Therefore, M = Rs. 750.
  The answer is D: Rs. 750.

Topic: Math
Question: I have a money pouch containing Rs. 700. There are equal number of 25 paise coins, 50 paise coins and one rupee coins.

Choices:
  A: 453

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 43 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The height of a room to its semi-perimeter is 2:5. It costs Rs.260 to paper the walls of the room with paper 50cm wide at Rs.2 per meter allowing an area of 15 sq.m for doors and windows. The height of the room is:
Choices:
  A: 2.6m
  B: 3.9m
  C: 4m
  D: 4.2m
  E: 4.4m
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the height of the room is 2x and the semi-perimeter is 5x.
  The perimeter of the room is 2 x semi-perimeter = 10x.
  The width of the room is (10x - 2 x 2x)/2 = 3x.
  The area of the room is 2x * 3x = 6x^2.
  The area of the doors and windows is 15 sq.m.
  The area of the walls is the area of the room - the area of the doors and windows = 6x^2 - 15.
  The length of the walls is the perimeter of the room times the height of the room = 10x * 2x = 20x^2.
  The cost of papering the walls is the length of the walls times the cost of the paper per meter = 20x^2 * 2/100 = 0.4x^2.
  We know that the cost of papering the walls is Rs.260, so 0.4x^2 = 260.
  Solving for x, we get x = 10.
  Therefore, the height of the room is 2x = 20.
  The answer is E: 4.4m.
Action: Answer("E")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume the height of the room is 2x and semi-perimeter is 5x.
  Then, the length of the room is 5x/2 - 2x = 9x/2.
  The area of the four walls is (2x)(9x/2) = 9x^2.
  The area of the doors and windows is given as 15 sq.m.
  The area of the four walls after deducting the area of doors and windows is 9x^2 - 15.
  The cost of papering the walls is Rs.260.
  The cost of papering one square meter of the wall is Rs.260/(9x^2 - 15).
  The width of the paper is 50cm = 0.5m and the cost of one meter of paper is Rs.2.
  Therefore, the cost of papering one square meter of the wall is Rs.4.
  So, we have Rs.4 = Rs.260/(9x^2 - 15).
  Solving this equation, we get 9x^2 - 15 = 65.
  Therefore, 9x^2 = 80 and x^2 = 80/9.
  Hence, the height of the room is 2x = 4x/2 = 4/3 * sqrt(80/9) = 4/3 * (4/3) * sqrt(5) = 16/9 * sqrt(5).
  Therefore, the answer is approximately 2.6 meters.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 2:
Thought:
  Let's assume the height of the room is 2x and the semi-perimeter is 5x.
  Then, the length of the room is 5x/2 - 2x = 9x/2.
  The area of the four walls is (2x)(9x/2) = 9x^2.
  The area of the doors and windows is 15 sq.m.
  The total area to be papered is 9x^2 - 15.
  The cost of papering is Rs.260.
  The cost of papering 1 meter of the wall is Rs.2.
  Therefore, the cost of papering 1 sq.m of the wall is Rs.0.04.
  So, (9x^2 - 15) * 0.04 = 260.
  Solving the above equation, we get x = 2.
  Therefore, the height of the room is 2x = 4m.
  The answer is C: 4m.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 44 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A man walks at 5 kmph for 6 hrs and at 4 kmph for 12 hrs. His average speed is
Choices:
  A: 4 1/3 km/h
  B: 7 2/3 km/h
  C: 9 ½ km/h
  D: 8 km/h
  E: 81 km/h
Response 0:
Thought:
  We can use the formula: Average speed = Total distance / Total time
  Let's calculate the total distance first.
  Distance walked at 5 kmph for 6 hours = 5 kmph x 6 hrs = 30 km
  Distance walked at 4 kmph for 12 hours = 4 kmph x 12 hrs = 48 km
  Total distance = 30 km + 48 km = 78 km
  Total time = 6 hrs + 12 hrs = 18 hrs
  Average speed = Total distance / Total time = 78 km / 18 hrs = 13/3 km/h
  Simplifying, we get 4 1/3 km/h
  Therefore, the answer is A: 4 1/3 km/h
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:

Question: The difference between the squares of two numbers is 256000 and the sum of the numbers is 1000. The numbers are
Choices:
  A: 600, 400
  B: 628, 372
  C: 640, 360
  D: None of these
  E: Cannot be determined
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the two numbers are x and y.
  According to the problem, we have two equations:
  x^2 - y^2 = 256000  (Equation 1)
  x + y = 1000        (Equation 2)
  We can use Equation 2 to solve for one of the variables in terms of the other, and then substitute into Equation 1 to solve for the other variable.
  From Equation 2, we have y = 1000 - x.
  Substituting into Equation 1, we get:
  x^2 - (1000 - x)^2 = 256000
  Simplifying and solving for x, we get:
  x = 628 or x = 372
  If x = 628, then y = 372
  If x = 372, then y = 628
  Therefore, the numbers are 628 and 372.
  The answer is B: 628, 372.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume the two numbers are x and y.
  According to the problem, we have two equations:
  x^2 - y^2 = 256000  (Equation 1)
  x + y = 1000        (Equation 2)
  We can use Equation 2 to solve for one of the variables, say y:
  y = 1000 - x
  We can substitute this into Equation 1 and simplify:
  x^2 - (1000 - x)^2 = 256000
  x^2 - (1000^2 - 2000x + x^2) = 256000
  -1000^2 + 2000x = 256000
  2x = 628
  x = 314
  We can substitute this back into Equation 2 to solve for y:
  y = 1000 - x = 686
  Therefore, the two numbers are 314 and 686.
  The answer is B: 628, 372.

  We also know that x + y = 1000.

  Substituting the values we know, we get (x+y)(x-y) = 256000.
  Substituting x+y = 1000, we get (1000)(x-y) = 256000.
  Solving for x-y, we get x-y = 256.
  Adding x+y = 1000 and x-y = 256, we get 2x = 1256.
  Solving for x, we get x = 628.
  Substituting x = 628 into x+y = 1000, we get y = 372.
  Therefore, the two numbers are 628 and 372.
  The answer is B: 628, 372.

    If x = 1200, then y = -200
  Since the second solution is not valid (we cannot have a negative number for y), the only solution is:
    x = 800 and y = 200
  Therefore, the answer is A: 600, 400.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 47 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A company produces 420 units of a particular computer component every month, at a production cost to the company of $110 per component, and sells all of the components by the end of each month. What is the minimum selling price per component that will guarantee that the yearly profit (revenue from sales minus production costs) will be at least $626,400 ?
Choices:
  A: 226
  B: 230
  C: 240
  D: 260
  E: 280
Response 0:
Thought:
  The company produces 420 units of a particular computer component every month.
  The production cost to the company of each component is $110.
  The yearly production cost is 420 * 12 * $110 = $554,400.
  The yearly profit should be at least $626,400.
  The yearly revenue should be $626,400 + $554,400 = $1,180,800.
  The minimum selling price per component that will guarantee the yearly profit will be at least $1,180,800 / (420 * 12) = $230.
  The answer is B: 230.
Action: Answer("B")

Question: If m > 0, y > 0, and x is m percent of 4y, then, in terms of y, m is what percentage of x?
Choices:
  A: y/400
  B: 4y
  C: 50y
  D: 2500/y
  E: 5000/y
Response 0:
Thought:
  If x is m percent of 4y, then x = (m/100)(4y) = 4my/100.
  We want to express m as a percentage of x, so we need to divide m by x and multiply by 100.
  m/x = m / (4my/100) = 100/4 = 25.
  Therefore, m is 25% of x.
  To express this in terms of y, we need to substitute x = 4my/100.
  m is 25% of x is equivalent to m = (25/100)(4my/100) = my/10.
  To express m as a percentage of x in terms of y, we need to divide m by x and multiply by 100, and substitute x = 4my/100.
  m/x = (my/10)/(4my/100) = 25/4.
  Therefore, m is (25/4)% of x in terms of y.
  We can simplify this as follows:
  (25/4)% = (25/4) * (1/100) = 1/16.
  Therefore, m is (1/16)x in terms of y.
  Substituting x = 4my/100, we get:
  m is (1/16)(4my/100) = my/400.
  Therefore, the answer is A: y/400.
Action: Answer("A")

Question: A sales person gets a 10% commission on each sale he makes. How many sales of $250 each must he make in order to reach a salary of at least $1000?

  A: 15
  B: 24
  C: 25
  D: 40
  E: 52

  We need to find the value of x that makes his total earnings at least $1000.
  So, we can set up an equation: 10% of 250x = $1000.
  Solving for x, we get x = 4.
  Therefore, the salesperson needs to make 4 sales of $250 each to reach a salary of at least $1000.

  Therefore, his total commission would be 10% of 250x, which is 25x.
  The question asks how many sales of $250 each must he make in order to reach a salary of at least $1000.
  Let's assume he makes y sales of $250 each to reach a salary of at least $1000.
  Therefore, his total commission would be 10% of 250y, which is 25y.
  We can set up an equation to solve for y: 25y >= 1000
  Solving for y, we get y >= 40.
  Therefore, the sales person must make at least 40 sales of $250 each to reach a salary of at least $1000.
  The answer is D: 40.

Question: A starts travel towards south 3km, then travel 5 km towards east, and again travels 3 km to north, and finally travels 2km towards west. In the end how far from is A from home?
Choices:
  A: 3km
  B: 2km
  C: 4km
  D: 5km
  E: 6km
Response 0:
Thought:
  A starts from a point and travels south 3km, which means A is 3km away from the starting point in the south direction.
  Then A travels 5km towards east, which means A is 5km away from the starting point in the east direction.

  Finally, A travels 2km towards west, which means A is 2km away from the starting point in the west direction.
  We can draw a diagram to visualize the path of A.
  
          N
          |
    W-----+-----E
          |
          S
  
  From the diagram, we can see that A has formed a right-angled triangle with sides of length 3km, 5km, and 2km.
  We can use the Pythagorean theorem to find the length of the hypotenuse, which is the distance of A from home.
  The Pythagorean theorem states that in a right-angled triangle, the square of the length of the hypotenuse is equal to the sum of the squares of the lengths of the other two sides.
  Therefore, the length of the hypotenuse is sqrt(3^2 + 5^2) = sqrt(9 + 25) = sqrt(34) km.
  The answer is sqrt(34) km, which is approximately 5.83 km.
  Therefore, the closest answer is D: 5km.

Question: Everyone in the family earns money each month. If the total income of a family per month is $9000 and the median income is $3000, how many members are there in the family?

  A: 2
  B: 3
  C: 4
  D: 5
  E: 6
Response 0:
Thought:
  The median income is the middle value of the incomes when they are arranged in order.
  If the median income is $3000, then there are incomes above and below this value.
  Let's assume there are 'n' members in the family.
  If we arrange the incomes in ascending order, then the median income will be the (n+1)/2th income.
  If the median income is $3000, then the sum of the incomes below $3000 is also $3000.
  The sum of all the incomes is $9000.
  Therefore, the sum of the incomes above $3000 is $3000 as well.
  So, the sum of all the incomes below and equal to $3000 is $3000*n/2.
  The sum of all the incomes above and equal to $3000 is $3000*n/2.
  Adding these two equations, we get $9000*n/2 = $9000.
  Solving for 'n', we get n = 3.
  Therefore, there are 3 members in the family.

Question: A starts a business with Rs.40,000. After 2 months, B joined him with Rs.60,000. C joined them after some more time with Rs.120,000. At the end of the year, out of a total profit of Rs.375,000, C gets Rs.150,000 as his share. How many months after B joined the business, did C join?
Choices:
  A: 2 months
  B: 4 months
  C: 23 months
  D: 24 months
  E: 84 months
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume C joined after x months.
  A invested for 12 months, B invested for (12-2) = 10 months, and C invested for (12-x) months.
  The ratio of their investments is 4:6:12 = 1:1.5:3
  Let's find the total profit share of A and B first.
  Total profit share of A and B = Total profit - Profit share of C = 375000 - 150000 = 225000
  Let's find the ratio of profit share of A and B.
  Ratio of profit share of A and B = Ratio of their investments = 1:1.5 = 2:3
  Let's assume the profit share of A and B are 2x and 3x respectively.
  Therefore, 2x + 3x = 225000
  5x = 225000
  x = 45000/5 = 9000
  Therefore, C joined after (12- x) = (12-9) = 3 months after B joined.
  The answer is not in the available choices. Therefore, the closest answer is B: 4 months.

Question: The monthly salary S of a shop assistant is the sum of a fixed salary of $500 plus 5% of all monthly sales. What should the monthly sales be so that her monthly salary reaches $1500?
Choices:

  B: $40000

  D: $20000

  Therefore, 500 + 0.05x = 1500.
  Solving for x, we get x = (1500 - 500) / 0.05 = 20000.
  Therefore, the monthly sales should be $20000.

Question: The sum of k consecutive integers is 51. If the least integer is -50, then k =
Choices:
  A: 40
  B: 62
  C: 82
  D: 92
  E: 102
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the k consecutive integers are x, x+1, x+2, ..., x+k-1.
  We know that the sum of these integers is 51.
  Therefore, we can write an equation as follows:
  x + (x+1) + (x+2) + ... + (x+k-1) = 51
  Simplifying the left-hand side of the equation, we get:
  kx + (1+2+...+(k-1)) = 51
  kx + (k-1)k/2 = 51
  kx + (k^2-k)/2 = 51
  k(2x+k-1) = 102
  We know that the least integer is -50, so x = -50.
  Substituting x = -50 in the above equation, we get:
  k(-100+k-1) = 102
  k^2 - 99k + 102 = 0
  Solving this quadratic equation, we get:
  k = 3 or k = 96
  We are looking for a positive value of k, so k = 96 is the answer.
  Therefore, the answer is D: 92.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 59 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A certain liquid passes through a drain at a rate of w/25 gallons every x seconds. At that rate, how many minutes will it take y gallons to pass through the drain?
Choices:
  A: y/(1200xy)
  B: 20xy/w
  C: 5xy/(12w)
  D: w/(3xy)
  E: 3y/(wx)
Response 0:
Thought:
  The liquid passes through the drain at a rate of w/25 gallons every x seconds.
  Therefore, the rate of the liquid is w/25 gallons per x seconds.
  To convert the rate to gallons per minute, we need to multiply by 60 seconds.
  So, the rate of the liquid is (w/25) * 60/x gallons per minute.
  To find how many minutes it will take y gallons to pass through the drain, we need to divide y by the rate of the liquid.
  Therefore, the time it will take is y / [(w/25) * 60/x] minutes.
  Simplifying the expression, we get (5xy) / (12w).
  Therefore, the answer is C: 5xy/(12w).
Action: Answer("C")

Topic: Math
Question: A square piece of cloth is trimmed by 4 feet on one edge to form a rectangular piece, which is then cut diagonally in half to create two triangles. If the area of each of triangle is 70 square feet, what was the perimeter (in feet) of the original piece of square cloth?
Choices:
  A: 56
  B: 58
  C: 60
  D: 62
  E: 64
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the original square piece of cloth has a side length of x feet.
  After trimming 4 feet from one edge, the new dimensions of the rectangular piece are (x-4) feet and x feet.
  The area of the rectangular piece is (x-4)x = x^2 - 4x square feet.
  The area of each triangle is 70 square feet, so the area of the rectangular piece is 2*70 = 140 square feet.
  Therefore, x^2 - 4x = 140.
  Rearranging the equation, we get x^2 - 4x - 140 = 0.
  Factoring the quadratic equation, we get (x-14)(x+10) = 0.
  Since x cannot be negative, x = 14.
  Therefore, the original square piece of cloth had a side length of 14 feet.
  The perimeter of the original square piece of cloth was 4x = 56 feet.
  The answer is A: 56.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume the original side of the square piece of cloth is x feet.
  After trimming 4 feet from one edge, the new dimensions of the rectangular piece are (x-4) by x.
  The area of the rectangular piece is (x-4) * x = x^2 - 4x.
  The area of each triangle is 70 square feet, so the area of both triangles is 140 square feet.
  The area of a triangle can be calculated as (1/2) * base * height.
  Since the two triangles are identical, the base and height of each triangle are equal.
  Let's assume the base and height of each triangle are y feet.
  The area of each triangle is (1/2) * y * y = 70.
  Solving for y, we get y = 2sqrt(35).
  The diagonal of the rectangular piece is the hypotenuse of the right triangle formed by the two identical triangles.
  The length of the hypotenuse can be calculated as sqrt((2y)^2 + (x-4)^2).
  Setting this equal to x, we get x^2 - 4x = 4y^2.
  Substituting y = 2sqrt(35), we get x^2 - 4x = 4 * 35 * 4.
  Solving for x, we get x = 14.
  Therefore, the perimeter of the original square piece of cloth is 4x = 56 feet.
  The answer is A: 56.

Topic: Math
Question: A rectangular parking space is marked out by painting three of its sides. If the length of the unpainted side is 9 feet, and the sum of the lengths of the painted sides is 37 feet, then what is the area of the parking space in square feet?
Choices:
  A: 46
  B: 81
  C: 126
  D: 252
  E: None
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the painted sides are the width and the length of the rectangle.
  Let's use "w" to represent the width and "l" to represent the length.
  The length of the unpainted side is 9 feet, so w = 9.
  The sum of the lengths of the painted sides is 37 feet, so 2l + w = 37.
  Substituting w = 9, we get 2l + 9 = 37, which gives us 2l = 28, and l = 14.
  Therefore, the area of the rectangle is lw = 9 x 14 = 126 square feet.
  The answer is C: 126.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the length of the painted sides is L and W.
  The length of the unpainted side is 9 feet.
  The sum of the lengths of the painted sides is 37 feet.
  Therefore, 2L + W = 37 and W = 37 - 2L.
  The area of the parking space is L x W x 9.
  Substituting W = 37 - 2L, we get A = 9L(37 - 2L).
  Expanding the equation, we get A = 333L - 18L^2.
  To find the maximum area, we need to find the value of L that maximizes A.
  Taking the derivative of A with respect to L, we get dA/dL = 333 - 36L.
  Setting dA/dL = 0, we get L = 9.25.
  Therefore, the maximum area is A = 333(9.25) - 18(9.25)^2 = 126.5625.
  Rounding to the nearest integer, the answer is 127.
Action: Answer("C")

Thought:

  We can solve for w by substituting l = 9 into the first equation: w + 2(9) = 37, so w = 19.
  Therefore, the area of the rectangle is w * l = 19 * 9 = 171 square feet.
  The answer is not "None of the above".

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 62 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Julie’s yard is rectangular. One side of the yard is 100 feet wide. The total area of the yard is 3,000 square feet. What is the length of the other side of the yard?
Choices:
  A: 30 feet
  B: 20 feet
  C: 10 feet
  D: 50 feet
  E: 60 feet
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the width of the yard is 100 feet.
  Let's use the formula for the area of a rectangle: A = l x w, where A is the area, l is the length, and w is the width.
  We know that the area of the yard is 3,000 square feet.
  We also know that one side of the yard is 100 feet wide.
  Therefore, we can solve for the length of the yard by dividing the area by the width: l = A / w.
  Substituting the values, we get l = 3,000 / 100 = 30 feet.
  Therefore, the length of the other side of the yard is 30 feet.
Action: Answer("A")

Thought:
  The area of a rectangle is the product of its length and width.

  Therefore, the length of the other side of the yard is 30 feet.

Topic: Math
Question: Hoses A and B spout water at different constant rates, and hose A can fill a certain pool in 8 hours. Hose A filled the pool alone for the first 2 hours and the two hoses, working together, then finished filling the pool in another 3 hours. How many hours would it have taken hose B, working alone, to fill the entire pool?
Choices:
  A: 8
  B: 15
  C: 12
  D: 6
  E: 3
Response 0:
Thought:
  Hose A fills the pool alone in 8 hours, so its rate is 1/8 of the pool per hour.
  Hose A filled the pool alone for the first 2 hours, so it filled 2/8 = 1/4 of the pool.
  The two hoses, working together, filled the remaining 3/4 of the pool in 3 hours.
  Let's say the rate of hose B is x, then the combined rate of the two hoses is (1/8 + x) of the pool per hour.
  Using the formula: rate x time = work, we can write the equation: 
  (1/8 + x) * 3 = 3/4
  Solving for x, we get x = 1/16.
  Therefore, hose B can fill the entire pool alone in 16 hours.
  The answer is not in the choices, but the closest answer is A: 8.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume that hose A can fill the pool in "a" hours and hose B can fill the pool in "b" hours.
  We know that hose A can fill the pool alone in 8 hours, so a = 8.
  In the first 2 hours, hose A filled 2/8 = 1/4 of the pool.
  In the next 3 hours, both hoses filled 3/x of the pool, where x is the total number of hours it took to fill the pool.
  We can set up an equation using the information above: 1/4 + 3/a + 3/b = 1
  We can simplify the equation to: 3/b = 1/2
  Therefore, hose B can fill the pool alone in 6 hours.
  The answer is D: 6.

Topic: Math
Question: Two numbers are in the ratio 3:5. If 9 is subtracted from each, the new numbers are in the ratio 12:23. The smaller number is?
Choices:
  A: 21
  B: 33
  C: 35
  D: 42
  E: 58
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let the two numbers be 3x and 5x.
  If 9 is subtracted from each, the new numbers are 3x-9 and 5x-9.
  According to the problem, (3x-9)/(5x-9) = 12/23.
  Cross-multiplying, we get 69x - 207 = 60x - 108.
  Solving for x, we get x = 99/3 = 33.
  Therefore, the smaller number is 3x = 3*33 = 99.
  The answer is B: 33.
Action: Answer("B")

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 65 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: If one of the roots of the quadratic equation x^2 + mx + 22 = 0 is 1.5, then what is the value of m?
Choices:
  A: -23.5
  B: -17.5
  C: -10.5
  D: -16.2
  E: Cannot be determined
Response 0:
Thought:
  We know that one of the roots of the quadratic equation is 1.5.
  Let's use the quadratic formula to solve for the other root and find the value of m.
  The quadratic formula is: x = (-b ± sqrt(b^2 - 4ac)) / 2a
  We can plug in the values from the given equation: x^2 + mx + 22 = 0
  a = 1, b = m, c = 22, and one of the roots, x = 1.5
  We can use x = 1.5 as one of the roots and solve for the other root:
  x = (-b ± sqrt(b^2 - 4ac)) / 2a
  1.5 = (-m ± sqrt(m^2 - 4(1)(22))) / 2(1)
  3 = -m ± sqrt(m^2 - 88)
  3 + m = sqrt(m^2 - 88) or 3 - m = sqrt(m^2 - 88)
  Squaring both sides of the equation:
  (3 + m)^2 = m^2 - 88 or (3 - m)^2 = m^2 - 88
  9 + 6m + m^2 = m^2 - 88 or 9 - 6m + m^2 = m^2 - 88
  6m = -97 or 12m = 97
  m = -97/6 or m = 97/12
  Since m must be negative, the only possible value is m = -97/6.
  Therefore, the answer is A: -23.5.
Action: Answer("A")

  Simplifying, we get:
  6m = -97 or 12m = 79
  Therefore, m = -97/6 or m = 79/12
  Since -97/6 is not one of the answer choices, the answer is D: -16.2

Response 4:
Thought:
  We know that one of the roots of the quadratic equation is 1.5.
  Let's use the quadratic formula to find the other root and solve for m.
  The quadratic formula is: x = (-b ± sqrt(b^2 - 4ac)) / 2a
  We can plug in the values from the equation x^2 + mx + 22 = 0:
  a = 1, b = m, c = 22, and x = 1.5
  We can solve for the other root by plugging in x = 1.5 and solving for b:
  1.5 = (-b ± sqrt(b^2 - 4ac)) / 2a
  Multiplying both sides by 2a:
  3a = -2b ± sqrt(b^2 - 4ac)
  Squaring both sides:
  9a^2 = 4b^2 - 4ac ± 4b sqrt(b^2 - 4ac) + 4ac
  Simplifying:
  9a^2 - 4b^2 + 4ac - 4ac = 4b sqrt(b^2 - 4ac)
  9a^2 - 4b^2 = 4b sqrt(b^2 - 4ac)
  Squaring both sides again:
  81a^4 - 72a^2b^2 + 16b^4 = 16b^2 (b^2 - 4ac)
  81a^4 - 72a^2b^2 + 16b^4 = 16b^4 - 64abc
  81a^4 - 72a^2b^2 = 48b^4 - 64abc
  81a^4 - 72a^2b^2 + 64abc - 48b^4 = 0
  Factoring out 8:
  8(9a^4 - 6a^2b^2 + 8abc - 6b^4) = 0
  We can see that the expression inside the parentheses is a perfect square:
  9a^4 - 6a^2b^2 + 8abc - 6b^4 = (3a^2 - 2b^2)^2 + 8abc - 8b^4
  Setting the expression inside the parentheses to zero:
  (3a^2 - 2b^2)^2 = 8b^4 - 8abc
  Taking the square root of both sides:
  3a^2 - 2b^2 = sqrt(8b^4 - 8abc)
  Solving for b:
  b = ±sqrt(22 - 3a^2)
  Since we know that one of the roots is 1.5, we can plug in x = 1.5 and solve for b:
  1.5^2 + m(1.5) + 22 = 0
  2.25 + 1.5m + 22 = 0
  1.5m = -24.25
  m = -16.17 (rounded to two decimal places)
  Therefore, the value of m is approximately -16.17.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 66 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In a large forest, 300 deer were caught, tagged, and returned during 2001. During 2002, 500 deer were caught at random, of which only 20 had tags from the previous year. If the percent of deer in the forest that had tags during the second year and were caught in the 500 deer sample is representative of the percent of the total deer population in the forest with tags, what is the total deer population in the forest (assuming no change in population between 2001 and 2002)?
Choices:
  A: 300
  B: 500
  C: 5000
  D: 6000
  E: 7500
Response 0:
Thought:
  The percent of deer in the forest that had tags during the second year and were caught in the 500 deer sample is representative of the percent of the total deer population in the forest with tags.
  During 2001, 300 deer were caught, tagged, and returned.
  During 2002, 500 deer were caught at random, of which only 20 had tags from the previous year.
  Therefore, the number of deer in the forest with tags during the second year is 300 + 20 = 320.
  Let x be the total deer population in the forest.
  Then, the percent of the total deer population in the forest with tags is (320/x)*100.
  We know that this percent is equal to the percent of deer in the 500 deer sample that had tags during the second year, which is (20/500)*100 = 4%.
  Therefore, we can write the equation (320/x)*100 = 4.
  Solving for x, we get x = (320*100)/4 = 8000.
  Therefore, the total deer population in the forest is 8000.
  The answer is E: 7500. 

Action: Answer("E")

  Therefore, 0.04x = 20.

  Therefore, the total deer population in the forest is 5000.
  The answer is C: 5000.

### Temperature: 2.0 | Problem 67 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In an exam, a candidate secured 504 marks of the maximum mark of M. If the maximum mark M is converted into 800 marks, he would have secured 420 marks. What is the value of M?
Choices:
  A: 278
  B: 2890
  C: 270
  D: 2702
  E: 960
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's use proportion to solve this problem.
  If the candidate secured 504 marks out of M, then his score as a fraction of M is 504/M.
  If the candidate secured 420 marks out of 800, then his score as a fraction of 800 is 420/800.
  We can set up a proportion: 504/M = 420/800.
  We can cross-multiply to get 504*800 = 420*M.
  We can solve for M by dividing both sides by 420: M = 504*800/420.
  We can simplify this expression by dividing the numerator and denominator by 4: M = 504*200/105.
  We can simplify further by dividing the numerator and denominator by 7: M = 72*40/3.
  Therefore, the value of M is 960.
Action: Answer("E")

  504/x = 420/800

  Therefore, the value of M is 960.

  E: 14

Therefore, the 3-digit number N can only be 1 or 1397.
The sum of the digits of 1 is 1, and the sum of the digits of 1397 is 20.
Since N cannot be 1, the answer is the sum of the digits of 1397 which is 20.
